Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talking Points

Wrongful Imprisonment Compensation Movement

— Chui

Going to court is originally the most unfortunate thing, and also the most painful thing. Regardless of criminal or civil cases, once involved in litigation, the outcome is difficult to predict. Even if one is fortunate enough to win the case, and the truth is revealed, the troublesome procedures and the burden of litigation costs are already considerable. Moreover, there are countless cases of prolonged litigation that lead to the parties' bankruptcy and ruin. Isn't litigation the most unfortunate and painful thing?

As the saying goes, "The government office opens wide, but those with reason and no money should not enter." Therefore, the darkness of judicial offices has been like this since ancient times. Han Shi Zhi said, "The law is for the common good of the world." Zhou Bo said, "I once commanded a million troops, how would I know the value of prison officials?" Therefore, according to the former saying, the law is a public instrument of the world, and judges should not arbitrarily manipulate it to distort the truth. According to the latter saying, under duress, nothing cannot be obtained; life and death are determined by the heart, and likes and dislikes are expressed through the mouth. What a terrifying authority!

Although it is said that judges originally have laws as their basis and facts as their standard, and cannot arbitrarily manipulate or reverse right and wrong, it should be known that the complexities of the matter and the application of the clauses all have the possibility of high and low considerations and arbitrary decisions. Therefore, in official documents of the past, there were two brilliant phrases: "The law is unforgiving, but the circumstances are excusable." With a single reversal, the severity of the crime can vary greatly. There were even cases of "killing with a knife" being changed to "swinging a knife to kill," with the difference between light and heavy being just a half-stroke. Although the laws have now been revised, there is still an absolute possibility of distorting the facts and making arbitrary decisions.

Therefore, if a judge cannot be upright and impartial and acts according to personal feelings, the suffering of the parties is truly "like a mute eating coptis, unable to express their bitterness." It goes without saying that if a judge is corrupt and perverts the law, distorting the truth, the judgment of the case will inevitably deviate from the principle of fairness. Even if they are ignorant of social conditions, do not understand the complexities of the case, and make arbitrary decisions, a wrongful case can be created. Or, if they pride themselves on their insight, conjecture the facts of the case, reverse right and wrong, and make arbitrary judgments, they can also create a wrongful case. In short, judicial officials should bear the heavy responsibility for unfair judgments caused by bribery. Even if a wrongful imprisonment is caused by carelessness or negligence, the judicial official cannot escape responsibility.

Although the judiciary is said to be independent, the authority of judges is not absolutely unlimited. They should bear considerable responsibility to the state and society. Judicial officials often misunderstand the meaning of judicial independence and the right to appeal, thinking that independence means they can freely make judgments. Even if an appeal results in vindication, the loss of reputation and material possessions is incalculable. If the judge bears no responsibility in such a situation, it is no wonder they act arbitrarily, with no regard for the consequences.

The doctrine of karma may not be enough to save the hearts of evildoers, but if a judge does not understand the suffering of the parties, is only interested in personal gain, and makes arbitrary judgments, causing one party to suffer injustice and be unable to vindicate the truth, those who accumulate resentment will surely bear the consequences.

Meeting the Ship

— Yun

Ying sent a telegram saying she had started her return to Shanghai from the southern country.

Calculating the dates, the ship should arrive today, but I dared not be certain, fearing a fruitless wait at the dock. So I went to the hotel to ask and was told that the ship would likely dock around five or six in the afternoon.

The early winter sun had already withdrawn its weak and feeble light, fleeing to the western horizon to rest. Although the cold wind was as sharp as a knife, making the ears and noses of those hurrying along blush like pigs' snouts, the joy of Ying's return after a year apart, along with our lovely, pure, and innocent child, made me feel not at all cold. I hurried to the Bund dock.

The dock was as noisy as ever. The porters' grunts of exertion were loud, fully expressing their strength. The melodious calls of the snack vendors and the laughter of the hotel greeters in their uniforms were so clamorous they could overwhelm one's senses.

The massive "Xinjiang" ship, like a small mountain, rested serenely beside the floating dock, its huge smokestack gently puffing out plumes of black smoke, allowing the porters to load goods into its belly.

Ah, this was the "Xinjiang" that took my Ying and our innocent, lively child away last year.

Then, the traces of past sorrow resurfaced in my heart.

It was during a hot summer day last year. I had lost my job and was living a vagrant life at sea. Economic hardship often caused our small family of three to worry about food and drink. I began to feel extremely miserable. Although the child often wore an innocent smile and affectionately coaxed me to laugh and hug him, I always felt that the child was too much of a burden. I cursed him for being born so early. But the child was innocent. He did not understand the inner turmoil of his father, who was weighed down by the burden of life. He always flashed a pair of dark, bright little eyes, revealing a natural smile. Sometimes, the child's incessant crying because he couldn't bear the hunger interrupted my train of thought and prevented me from writing, arousing my anger. I would angrily spank the child's buttocks. As a result, Ying became dissatisfied and argued with me, lying stiffly on the bed and sobbing.

Finally, one evening, the dark sky was studded with dense stars, and fireflies lit torches to enter the children's dreams, flying from one dark corner to another, luring the children to chase and shout. On that summer evening, Ying, holding the child, sat with me under the eaves, enjoying the cool air. After a moment of contemplation, Ying said to me very seriously:

"Ren, our life is so precarious now that we can hardly survive, especially for the child. I think I should take the child back to the South. This way, I can lessen your burden and allow you to work in peace." Ying's voice trembled, and I guessed she must be crying in the dark.

"I think it's better not to go. This kind of life won't last long anyway. Ying, is it?" The thought of Ying leaving made my heart ache a little. However, the instability of life over the years made me feel too sorry for Ying and the child.

"No, it's better for me to go. Maybe I can find some work to do in the South," Ying replied without hesitation and with certainty.

So Ying and our innocent child were taken away by this "Xinjiang" ship.

The darkness of night had already fallen upon the earth, blurring all the distant scenes across the river. At this time, the pier's lights had already shone with brightness. My heart began to feel a little anxious. I turned to the partners who had come to meet their people and asked:

"Why hasn't the ship come alongside the dock yet?"

"It might have to stop outside Wusongkou tonight," the partners answered indifferently, rubbing the backs of their hands, scattering like birds returning to the forest.

I felt utterly disappointed. At the same time, the icy cold wind assaulted my thin autumn coat, making me shiver uncontrollably. Finally, I quickly left the noisy dock and returned home with a disappointed heart.

The Meaning of Life

— Bu Bai

Old Friend:

We all saw the film "The Ordeal of the Peach and Plum"! After you left the Jin Cheng Grand Theatre, didn't you say this: "I'm actually afraid of life! I'm shrinking!" I didn't say anything to you at the time. We walked silently, walked on.

Page 18

I was thinking; that male protagonist in the film, in order to survive, was demoted from a shipping company employee to a worker in a construction factory, and then fell further, becoming a thief, and was eventually shot dead for resisting arrest! Ah! Indeed, how could this not make you afraid of life? Shrink?

Thinking, walking silently, we eventually separated at the crossroads. Turning my head back, I saw the backs of you and your lover. I shook my head and sighed at your backs.

Alas! Old friend! You are afraid of life. You are like a vibrant flower, withered by the cold winter wind! How pitiful!

Today, I suddenly received your letter, inviting me to talk. During our conversation, I realized how distressed you are! You don't want to return to your corrupt family, but you also don't have the courage to rent a small room and live the "wild rose" life you admire. Because you say; it's quite inconvenient, such as boiling water and all sorts of chores.

But old friend! You sighed again after all; "I'm afraid of life! I'm shrinking!"

Old friend! Here, you have too much of a misunderstanding of the meaning of "life"! You think that anything that requires "struggle" is life, but old friend! Your understanding of life is wrong. In this very mistake, you lack the heart of "advancement"!

Life, yes life, from the moment an infant comes into the world from its mother's womb, it has to live. Life is always in need of "struggle." Without the strength to "struggle" against the environment, then there will be no life. Without life, wouldn't that person become someone in a grave? Therefore, every person always has "life," which is to say, they have at least "more or less" strength to struggle. Being afraid of life, in the end, will inevitably be killed by the environment!

Old friend! This way, you are "living," which is to say you are struggling for life! But old friend! Forgive me for being so blunt in criticizing you, you lack the courage to "move forward" too much, and you also think that only "struggling" is life, therefore, you are afraid of a life of struggle. Little do you know that you are living now, aren't you also struggling at every moment?

I've said too much! Do you find it annoying? In one sentence, you lack the courage to "move forward" too much.

Finally, you must understand that a young person of a new era must have the spirit of "self-criticism." We must constantly examine ourselves, we must constantly urge ourselves! Why? Because we are deeply afraid that we will "turn backwards!"

Life is struggle! Only struggle is life! I wish you to move forward!

Musings by the Stove

— Xiaolin

The weather is getting cold, which is a threat to us poor folks. The north wind is blowing all day outside, and the sun is hiding in the clouds, not even bothering to show its face. In times like these, it's perfect for the rich to indulge their pleasures. Changes in the weather have no effect on them. On the contrary, the different seasons give them a more flavorful and pleasant mood. In such freezing winters, if it happens to be snowing outside the window, the scenery becomes even more beautiful. They are wrapped up in warm, luxurious, radiator-heated rooms, only needing to wear a thin shirt to appreciate the silver world of snow outside. Perhaps they even turn on the radio, playing a few cheesy songs, indulging in a particularly poetic winter day. If they happen to be in the mood, they can easily jump into their car and drive out to the suburbs to watch the snow.

We poor folks don't have such blessings. Right now, we can only close our eyes and admire them in our fantasies. Sometimes, even the right to fantasize feels very precious. Because as soon as we open our eyes, the troubles of reality immediately swarm our minds. In front of us is a small iron stove - which we can pretend is a radiator. We put in a few pieces of black coal to get some warmth. Besides that, there's a bag of peanuts and a bowl of yellow wine. We slowly sip the wine, nibble on the peanuts, and watch the flames rise in the stove. Thinking about it, being able to spend winter days like this can also be considered comfortable. People should know when to stop and be content. Why be extravagant? A few cups of yellow wine and a pile of peanuts, the light flavor also has a not-so-light meaning. If we feel too lonely staying in the room alone, then we can call a few more people over. If there are more people, and they all like to drink, then we add some wine and some snacks. Everyone gathers around the stove, the red light of the fire makes everyone's face feel warm. The faces that were already a little red from the wine become even redder. Then, everyone talks and laughs, all with a bit of alcohol in them, and are more excited than usual. Some people, without any reservation, tell their sweet love stories that they usually wouldn't want to talk about, and the listeners also find it quite interesting. But there's no need to turn on the radio and play a few popular songs. So those who are good at singing start singing themselves, which is more intimate and moving. In this kind of situation, with wine, songs, and laughter, time passes by very pleasantly.

But suddenly, there's a moment of silence. After the silence, talking about this and that, somehow we start talking about ourselves. Once we start talking about ourselves, the energy that everyone just had disappears in an instant. The air immediately becomes very stuffy, as if it's about to solidify. Everyone is silent, silently lowering their heads. No one wants to say a word, and everyone is trapped in their own worries and falls into the web of煩惱. Besides a faint sigh, there's only the crackling sound from the stove. Why did everyone suddenly become so dejected? This is something that no one wants to say! Just let each person know it in their heart. We also have the same feeling. What we sigh for is that even these ordinary days are not easy to get through, and we are all gritting our teeth and holding on.

What else is there to be happy about? Aren't we just borrowing temporary intoxication to temporarily numb the pain? But the pain often doesn't disappear because of this. Instead, the pain becomes even more unbearable.

Until the middle of the night, everyone is a bit tired. We see them out the door. We return to our small, freezing room. The fire in the stove has gradually weakened, and there are only a few pieces of coal left. It probably won't last through half the night. And at this time, the snow is falling harder. We worry that on their way back, they might catch a cold since the alcohol they drank earlier hasn't completely worn off. What if they get sick tomorrow? But when we touch our pockets, we only have a few coppers left. There's no way to add more coal, and even next year's livelihood is uncertain. The alcohol wears off early, and the warmth on our body also fades. Thinking about it, our feelings and limbs also become cold. We blindly crawl into bed, and let everything be said about it tomorrow!

— Yuyan

A Mother's Tears

— Ya Fei

Flow, flow, flow, endlessly flowing; a mother's tears are inexhaustible!

What I fear most is seeing my mother's tears, because every time I see them, I feel uneasy and ashamed; yet she often sheds them in front of me. But why does she weep? And how can I stop her from weeping? Alas, it truly makes me feel infinitely ashamed!

Perhaps it's because I'm not progressing enough! Having raised such a big son, she still has to toil and run around, unable to enjoy a peaceful day. Logically speaking: she's so old, her son is so grown up! The daughter-in-law is already married into the family, and the grandson is already held in her arms. To most people, this would seem like a wonderful blessing; but, but she has no blessing, only grievances! I am truly laden with sin!

My mother has become even older and thinner in recent years, and her cough has become worse than in previous years. Yet she still has such a competitive spirit, always unwilling to let young people take a step forward. Seeing her son – me – in dire straits, with expenses growing daily while income dwindles, she worries about me greatly. Therefore, she always tries heaven and earth to help me produce something. Moreover, I have suffered a massive blow in recent years after the rural bankruptcy!

However, the nature of our mother-son relationship differs from the "benevolent mother and filial son" situation of others. As long as we are together, we quarrel, eventually escalating from arguments to disputes. She likes to nag, while I am inherently irritable. Both of us are equally stubborn. After each quarrel, she refuses to eat, lies in bed, and weeps. At that time, I also hide in bed and weep: the internal contradictions torment me. I regret that I shouldn't have clashed with her. But when idle words reach my lips, they can't be taken back, and there's no time to weigh their importance. After a day, we comfort each other again, but after a while, we clash again at the slightest disagreement. I am truly an unfilial son! She helps me so much, why can't I even concede a single word? I curse myself, why can't I understand her?

I remember the first time I returned home after graduating. At that time, I was as happy as if I had passed the imperial examination and returned home in glory by imperial decree. A few days before setting off, I wrote a letter home to tell my mother when I would return. From then on, I eagerly hoped for the day of my return to come quickly. My heart truly felt like "my heart returns like an arrow!" But the days seemed to pass especially slowly, as if deliberately opposing me. At night, I don't know how many beautiful dreams I had of returning home, dreaming of how happy my mother would be to see me return, laughing with happiness, tears streaming down her face.

Back home, I quarreled with her again the next day; so after three days, I returned to the shop. This time I cried for three whole days, and cried so sadly that I became weak. When I got to the shop, I cried heartily again. I have never been willing to put up with grievances in my life.

The day before yesterday, my mother came to Shanghai, and I quarreled with her again. When we quarreled, she shed tears. I couldn't bear to see her tears, but I couldn't stop her from shedding them. Later, I came back and secretly shed tears all night myself. The next night, I wanted to send her to the train, but she had already left quietly. Disappointed and grieving, I wandered around the station for three hours, returning home late at one in the morning. Alas! I am too heartless. I should kneel before the cross to be punished!

Amateur Letter Box

Explanation Regarding Volcanoes

Mr. Editor:

I now have a question about natural science that I would like to ask you to answer.

I often see news reports about volcanic eruptions in various countries, which I find very strange. What causes volcanoes? Why do they erupt? I have asked many people, but their answers are very vague and unclear, which makes me even more suspicious. Therefore, I am writing this letter to you, hoping that you can fulfill my expectations! Best wishes,

Wang Yue, respectfully

Editor's Note: Although we do not have much research on natural science issues, if readers have such questions, we will do our best to answer them based on what we know, or refer them to experts for answers. We always want readers to gain a relatively clear understanding.

How do volcanoes erupt? This is indeed a very interesting question. To those who do not know,

Page 19

it must seem very strange and mysterious, but after careful research by scientists, we can know that this is just a natural phenomenon in the universe.

To talk about the causes of volcanoes, we must delve into the internal structure of the earth. We have not yet gained a clear understanding of the internal structure of the earth, because we currently lack excellent and complete instruments to see into the Earth's core. However, according to scientists' speculation, the causes of volcanic formation and eruption are likely due to water vapor and heat. Some say that since the Earth was formed from extremely hot gases, the interior must still retain a very high temperature. Others believe that heat is generated by friction when the Earth's layers move. Since the discovery of radioactive materials, some have also believed that the Earth is formed by the disintegration of atoms of various elements. Volcanoes are the same. Although it is not yet possible to determine who is right and who is wrong, based on general common sense, we can believe that the interior of the Earth does indeed contain a very high temperature. At the same time, magma cannot solidify and is constantly compressed by the Earth's crust. Naturally, it has a large swelling force. Once the Earth's crust is eroded and loosened by the outside world, it is bound to be burst open, and the magma is bound to seize the opportunity to rush out. This is the so-called common explanation of volcanoes.

Volcanic eruptions can be violent or gentle. Generally, volcanoes that erupt frequently are mostly gentle. Volcanoes that have been dormant for a long time and then erupt are mostly violent; and the longer the dormancy period, the more violent the eruption. When violent volcanoes erupt, they stir up huge waves in the sea, overturning ships; the coast also shakes extremely violently, and many houses are destroyed. The casualties of humans and animals are even more horrifying. The situation at that time is truly terrifying. However, there are very few volcanoes within China. Most are in the Americas and Japan in the Pacific basin.

News: The Shanghai Literary Friends Association is scheduled to hold its third annual gathering on the 25th of this month at the Nanjing Hotel (Basin Soup Alley). In addition to a dinner for members of the headquarters and branch offices, association members Lin Yin, Zhou Tianlai, Chen Liang, Zhu Shaofei, Wang Zhuo, Wu Chengda, etc. will perform various programs, which will be very interesting. There will also be many gifts for distribution on the spot as souvenirs. Non-members are welcome to join the gathering. The cost of the meal is one dollar and fifty cents. A special issue has been printed; a copy will be sent immediately upon request. Correspondence address: 480 Fuzhou Road.

"Falling Rosy Clouds and Lonely Wild Ducks"

Luoxia suddenly got scarlet fever, which worried Jiang Qiuwu, who hurriedly sent Luoxia to the hospital. Because the doctor said that the patient was in danger, Jiang Qiuwu stayed in the hospital overnight. The next day, Luoxia's condition took a turn for the better, and Qiuwu was relieved to go home: as soon as he entered the house, Feng Yuru was sitting alone in the room. Yuru knew that Luoxia was sick, so she replaced Luoxia to fulfill her wife's duties. At this time, Jiang Qiuwu had special feelings traveling in his mind!

Huamei (1060) 10:00 PM to 11:00 PM

"Man Jiang Hong"

Qin Xiaoxiang stole Bai Zhengxiu's money and a diamond ring and hurriedly fled home. She saw Bai Zhengxiu's car at her door. She knew that this matter must have been discovered. She was at a loss for a while, and suddenly thought of Taozhi, so she hurriedly went to find Taozhi. She met Li Taihu on the road. Taihu saw Xiaoxiang in such a panic, so he secretly followed Xiaoxiang to Li Taozhi's house. Taihu completely heard what Xiaoxiang and Taozhi said. Taihu was willing to guarantee Qin Xiaoxiang, so he broke into Li Taozhi's house.

Ms. Wang Bingmei's Tang Poetry

Huaxing (1260) 9:00 AM to 10:00 AM

Spring Grievance Liu Fangping

The setting sun gradually turns to dusk at the silk window, no one in the golden house sees the tear stains.

Lonely, empty courtyard, spring is about to end, pear blossoms cover the ground, the door is not opened.

Grievance of a Soldier Liu Fangping

Year after year, the Golden River returns to Yuguan, morning after morning, the horsewhip and the knife ring.

Three springs of white snow return to the Qing Tomb, ten thousand miles of the Yellow River wind around the Black Mountain.

Palace Poem Liu Fangping

The sound of Sheng and song rises halfway in the jade building, the wind sends the laughter of the palace ladies.

The shadow of the moon palace opens, hearing the night leak, the crystal curtain rolls up near the autumn river.

Hearing the Flute on the Night of Ascending the Surrender City Li Yi

The sand in front of Huile Peak is like snow, the moon outside the surrender city is like frost.

I don't know where to blow the reed pipe, all the soldiers look towards their homeland all night.

Wuyi Lane Liu Yuxi

Wild grass flowers by the Vermilion Bird Bridge, the setting sun slants at the entrance of Wuyi Lane.

The swallows in front of the halls of the old Wang and Xie families fly into the homes of ordinary people.

Spring Poem Liu Yuxi

New clothes are suitable for the face, descending the Zhu Gui, treasuring and locking up the spring light, a courtyard of sorrow.

Walking to the middle of the courtyard, counting the flower buds, a dragonfly flies onto the jade hairpin.

Shenbao Architecture Weekly

Outline of the Traffic Ministry Building Construction

— A-Shou

The Traffic Ministry Building, which took four and a half years to construct, has recently opened for public viewing this month. Its majestic grandeur and sophisticated, practical facilities surpass those of any other building in the capital. While the Chinese White House (National Government), the Railway Ministry, the Foreign Ministry, and other government agencies are indeed refined and grand, they pale in comparison to the Traffic Ministry, resembling small sorcerers before a great one.

Located north of the capital city, at the southern end of Sajiawan, and facing the Railway Ministry to the east and west, the square-shaped building occupies fifty acres of land and cost approximately 2,000,000 yuan to construct. Construction began in 1931 under the former Minister of Transportation, Wang Boqun, who signed a contract with Xin Fengji and commissioned a Russian architect to design the blueprints. However, the September 18th Incident of the same year led to the suspension of construction. Later, under the leadership of the current Minister of Transportation, Zhu Jiaju, the project was diligently promoted and continued, resulting in the magnificent new building that graces the capital and stands superior to all other structures in the new capital.

The exterior of the building exudes splendor, solemnity, and tranquility. The design incorporates both Chinese and Western palace styles. The main entrance faces Zhongshan Road and features two gates, north and south, approximately thirty yards apart, connected by a short wall. The perimeter of the building is surrounded by a ring wall and a protective moat, with flowing clear water, adding a unique charm. Stone bridges span the river for passage and provide a grand view. Inside the main gate, the right side houses the information room, while the left side serves as the guard room. Each section is adorned with exotic flowers, beautiful grasses, verdant trees, and elegant plants.

The new building consists of four interconnected floors. The central section comprises two four-story buildings, topped with a small pavilion and a rooftop garden. Flanking the main building are two three-story structures, reportedly housing the General Post Office and the Directorate General of Telecommunications. The building has a total of four entrances. The odd-numbered entrances (first and third) are palace-style pavilion gates, while the even-numbered entrances are city gate-style arched doorways. Behind the gates are gardens connecting to the rear building. The interior comprises over three hundred rooms, including offices for various departments and bureaus, facing each other and standing opposite one another. Windows all face outward. The walls are constructed of cement, smooth and clean. The office floors are made of pine wood, coated with bronze-colored paint, creating a bright and inviting atmosphere. The walls are painted white, while the walls of the minister and vice-minister's offices are decorated with green wallpaper with gold trim. The allocation of rooms on each of the four floors is largely complete. The ground floor houses the general affairs department, technical offices, and a dining hall. The second floor contains the offices of the minister and vice-ministers, as well as the secretariat, the counselors' office, the navigation department, and the auditorium. The third floor houses the offices of the postal department, the telecommunications department, and the employee affairs committee. The fourth floor houses the accountant-general's office and the library. The second floor is considered the essence of the entire building. The auditorium is vast and spacious, supported by six large vermilion wooden pillars. The ceiling is intricately carved and features eye-catching green and gold color combinations, complementing each other. The floor is made of high-quality Western wooden strips, pieced together to form various patterns, adding splendor and beauty, enhancing the reputation of Chinese architecture. The broad and practical stage can be used for dancing and banquets, as well as for theatrical performances. The hall has around a thousand leather seats and can accommodate at least seven hundred people.

The minister's office is located on the second floor of the rear building, occupying three large rooms and one small room. The rooms are divided into an office, a dressing room, a large reception room, and a small reception room. The office is exquisitely decorated and furnished, with everything needed. The desk has three telephones, a rarity compared to other ministries. The vice-minister's office is located on the second floor of the front building, with similar facilities to the minister's office, except for the absence of a reception room.

Other equipment in the various rooms, such as desks and chairs, are all Western-style. Electricity, heating, electric bells, telephones, and wireless radios are all the latest 20th-century installations. The electric lights, telephones, and wireless radios are supplied by Siemens, while the electric bells are installed in the walls. The telephones can be used in three ways: (1) automatic communication with ministry personnel for official business; (2) external communication; and (3) prioritizing urgent matters without interrupting ongoing conversations. This type of facility is unprecedented in government agencies in the capital. Furthermore, the new building offers the convenience of conducting ministry meetings and discussions via telephone, eliminating the need to gather everyone in one room, thereby increasing work efficiency. It is said that the Ministry of Transportation's relocation is well underway, and the General Post Office will move its operations from Shanghai to Beijing in January of next year. It is also rumored that the construction funds for the new Ministry of Transportation building were drawn from the surplus of the Postal Savings and Remittances Bureau.

General Situation of Capital Construction (Continued)

— Yang Dehui

In the past, Nanjing's construction was very depressed due to population reasons. The development of Nanjing's construction after the capital was established is self-evident. According to the statistics of the Public Works Bureau, the construction in the past four years has been progressing gradually. The construction area, number of projects, and cost from 1931 to June of this year are written below. In 1931, the land area occupied by residential construction was 46,740 square meters, the construction cost was 7,149,495 yuan, and there were 1,034 projects. In 1932, the construction occupied 90,855 square meters, the cost was 3,911,352 yuan, and there were 665 projects. In 1933, the construction area was 23,775 square meters, the cost was 3,084,381 yuan, and there were 751 projects. In the first six months of this year, the construction area was 11,332 square meters and the cost was 4,206,034 yuan, and there were 417 projects. In the past three years and six months, the total construction area was 172,702 square meters, the cost was 18,351,262 yuan, and there were 2,867 projects. As for those renovated and rebuilt buildings, they are not included. From the above amount, the general situation of the current construction can be imagined.

Before Nanjing became the capital, most of the buildings were concentrated in the east and west of the city. In the north of the city, except for the official residences, consulates, and the self-built foreign-style buildings of one or two wealthy people, most of them were low houses and thatched huts where poor people lived. There was no construction to speak of, so it was not easy to find neat residences. After the capital was established, due to the daily increase of the population, the small number of residences in Nanjing could not accommodate this huge population. A few years ago, we could still see barren land and ponds. Now, many of them have become construction sites for high-rise buildings. For example, Huiyuanli, Jintangli, Liangyouli, Wenhuali, Zhonglinfang, Zijinfang, Zhongyifang, Wutaishan Village, Meiyuan New Village, Taoyuan New Village...etc. are all new buildings on the former barren land and ponds. Moreover, in each of these villages and neighborhoods, there are dozens or even hundreds of houses. Other small-scale construction projects are too numerous to mention. As for private residential construction, the number is also quite large! With Nanjing's land area of 477.845 square kilometers, compared with the current population and construction, it is obviously not very crowded. However, Nanjing already has zoning regulations, which are divided into six districts: (1) Central Political District, (2) Cultural District, (3) Urban Garden District, (4) Residential District, (5) Commercial District, (6) Industrial District. Although the boundaries have not yet been precisely determined, they will certainly be determined in the future. Because if the city is not divided into districts, the construction will inevitably be mixed, which will be a great hindrance to the lives of citizens and the entire city. Therefore, the Nanjing city government has already paid attention to dividing the six districts, and the residential area is located near Gulou in the north of the city and in the northwest of the city, starting from Xihuamen and along Zhongshan Road. As mentioned above, the north of the city was a very desolate place with no construction to speak of before the capital was established. Now, because it is designated as a residential area, construction has increased a lot in the past few years to accommodate the influx of people. The future expansion is just around the corner.

Because the population of Nanjing is increasing day by day, the soaring prices of real estate are an inevitable trend. In the past, the land that was worthless is now very expensive. According to the land prices approved by the Finance Bureau recently, the general situation of land prices in Nanjing can also be seen. Guo Jiaqiao outside Hepingmen sells for 1,690 yuan per square, the land behind Zhonghua Road is valued at 4,000 yuan per mu, Zhongshan Road is valued at more than 10,000 yuan per mu, Chibi Road in the residential area is valued at 5,000 yuan per mu, Zhongzheng Road is valued at 120 yuan per square, Youshi Avenue is valued at 25,600,000 yuan per mu, Jianye Road is valued at 3,000 yuan per mu, Guofu West Street is valued at 56,000 yuan per mu, Huiyuanli in the north of the city is valued at 100 yuan per square, and Zhongshan Road is valued at 12,300 yuan per mu. In short, land prices are rising sharply year by year, just like the construction industry. Since land prices are so high, housing has become a serious problem for residents. Because of the increase in urban population and the soaring land prices, the rent is rising day by day, which is a chain reaction. In the past, the rent in Nanjing was very cheap. If you spent dozens of yuan a month, you could rent a decent residence. Now, it has exceeded the rent price of four or five times years ago, and the deposit is large, more than three or five times the rent, or even seven or eight times. This phenomenon further proves that the supply of housing is insufficient. As a result, people pay a high price, but the accommodation they get is just like a birdcage. For example, in the newly built villages and neighborhoods in the north of the city, the rooms are not very spacious or comfortable. Living alone in a house is already very cramped, and the rent is as high as 40 to 100 yuan per month. Therefore, the general residents spend 20% to 30% of their monthly income on rent, and the houses they live in are still closed. The people living around them are very close together. As a result of this kind of living, not only does it have a significant impact on the national economy, but it also leads to physical weakness and mental fatigue. The various intangible losses are very significant. Therefore, the municipal authorities, in view of the daily increase in population, should consider the necessity of low-income housing to solve the housing problem in Nanjing. Finally, the future construction of Nanjing, along with the consolidation of politics, is just beginning to flourish! (The End)

Architectural Jargon (II)

— Mei Zhenhuan

丨丨 Regarding usage in the construction site 丨丨

Cloud Strip 丨丨 It is a planed wooden strip, approximately one inch wide and six tenths of an inch thick. It is commonly used by plasterers for plastering work, whether it be for drawing lines for ceiling molding (HorseofMoulding), applying fine sand, or panel lines, etc. It has a wide range of applications.

Scraping Ruler 丨丨 It is the work after the bricks are laid. That is, plastering. Usually, straw mud (Strawmud) is used as the base. (Straw mud is a mixture of straw, black sand, and lime slurry.) Initially, a cloud strip is used to even out the thickness of the wall surface, then straw mud is applied, and then a scraping ruler is used to smooth it out.

Horse 丨丨 It is a type of template derived from a detail (an architect enlarges a part of the drawing, called a detail) used when plastering ceiling moldings. It is made of five or six tenths of an inch thick wood and is called a horse.

White Ground 丨丨 (Shank) It is the flat surface in the middle of the dentil and the fluted sides of a Doric architrave. It is called the white ground.

Dentil 丨丨 It is a type of decoration in plastering work. It is usually used on elaborate ceiling cornices near the wall. They are small pieces with white ground in between that are glued on. There is no fixed pattern for its design.

Layer Stick 丨丨 (LayerstickorCourespole) It is a planed wooden rod (approximately four inches square). There are black marking lines drawn on the surface. These lines indicate the distance between the bricks and the mortar joints. It is generally used on fair-faced brick walls to prevent the long seams from being skewed or curved.

Long Seam 丨丨 (Horizotedjoist) Each mortar joint (Pointing) that runs horizontally as bricks are laid is called a long seam. Conversely, a vertically discontinuous joint is called a head seam (Verticaljoist).

Header Brick 丨丨 The width of a brick (Headbrick) is called the header. Its length is called a stretcher brick (Strectcbetbrick). Plasterers have a method called header-stretcher bond, which is a method of laying bricks by alternating headers and stretchers.

New Number Three 丨丨 What is called New Number Three? It is a nickname for a type of brick. Its dimensions are nine and one-tenth inches long, four and a half inches wide, and one and six-tenths of an inch thick. There is also a type called Number Three Fang, which measures eight and seven-tenths inches, four and two-tenths inches, and one and six-tenths inches. Both blue and red are available. However, there are several nicknames for bricks. The most common production areas are Xiadian Temple, Hongjiatan, and Luxu. However, currently, Taishan, Zhensu, Dazhong, and other brands are widely used in various construction sites. (To be continued)

Talking About the Design of Wine Dance Halls (Part Two)

— Pillow Wood

Regarding the interior 丨丨, this refers to the structure inside the walls and gates of the wine dance hall. The following should be noted: (1) Dance floor: Dancing is a related business in wine dance halls, so a dance floor must be designed. (2) For the convenience of female customers, a dressing and washing room should be set up. (3) The allocation of indoor space must be carefully considered. (4) The staircase leading to the large kitchen should be long and wide, and well-lit to facilitate movement. (5) The upper floors can be decorated with calligraphy, paintings, flowers, curtains, etc. (6) It is okay to place thicker columns in the dining room; the main kitchen can sometimes be divided into countless small dining rooms, but the partitions of such dining rooms should have soundproof double walls to facilitate the privacy of customers. (7) Sometimes, to accommodate group or family customers, they can be designed in the style of apartments, with living rooms, private washrooms, dining rooms, etc. for service. (8) If possible, the design of a rooftop garden is also necessary. (9) Regarding the stove room and the cooking room, they must be properly located to save time. For example, the oven and wine cellar can be set up on the lower floor of the main kitchen.

Regarding the exterior 丨丨, this is only the appearance of the main entrance and wall decorations. The solemnity, timeliness, attractiveness, novelty, and eye-catching colors should all be taken into consideration. The windows facing the street should also be designed to be mysterious and attractive, and new decorations should be prepared frequently to promote awareness. The entrance and exit doors must be flexible to open and close, and their width should be at least wide enough for four or five people to walk in and out side by side. Rotating glass push doors can also be used.

(B) Construction In the design of wine dance halls, the construction aspects can be divided into: air, elevators, light, telephone, wireless radio, etc.: (1) The air in the house is very important, and it must be designed to circulate to prevent smog. (2) The design of the elevator must be new, safe, and fast. In addition to transporting people, it can also transport food directly up and down. (3) Light in wine dance halls is related to dancing and music, so it must be designed appropriately. (4) The telephone in the wine dance hall is used by many people and should be disinfected frequently, and the location of the telephone room should be in a central area for easy access. (5) Wireless radios in wine dance halls can be included as an auxiliary entertainment.

(C) Exterior View When designing a wine dance hall, it is best to have a garden outside, so that customers who are drunk can feel refreshed after going out, and it is especially needed in the hot summer.

(D) Decoration and Furniture In the construction of furniture and decorations in wine dance halls, lampshades can be added to the lamps, mirrors can be inlaid on the walls, and small lamps can be specially prepared for dancing. Copper handrails, aluminum chair backs, and silver countertops can add a lot of color and excitement.

The above are the important points for the design of wine dance halls. In addition, the height of the tables that should be placed in the wine dance hall should be 30 inches. The table top for two people should be 30 x 30 inches, and the table top for four people should be 36 x 36 inches. The allocation of tables in each room should be 50% for two-person tables, 30% for four-person tables, and the remaining 20% for round tables. This is also introduced here for your attention. (The End)

Shenbao Local Supplement Film Special

"Suffering the Most Bitter Hardships Leads to Being the Best" (Part Two)

— Mitong

Today's stars are yesterday's extras

Don't be discouraged, hard work is the path to success

There must be tens of millions of women around the world who admire and envy Joan Crawford. They always like to say, "If only I had her opportunity, I could be rich for a while." They imitate Joan's hairstyle, they imitate Joan's clothes, they imitate Joan's lipstick, and they imitate her every move. They don't know that every woman has a better chance of success than Joan, because Joan's rise to stardom is not based on her appearance. Her rise step by step comes from work, learning, hard work, and persistence. When she was extremely tired and her muscles and bones ached all over, she still gritted her teeth and finished practicing dancing. She understood her lack of knowledge. When her eyes were swollen from the mercury lights, she still studied hard on her own without interruption. When she was an extra, she never loafed around like other extras. When she was in the photography studio, she imitated the style of big stars. When she got home, she performed in front of the mirror. The mirror was her unyielding and un-flattering teacher. She analyzed and dissected herself like a biologist dissecting a new specimen. She relentlessly sought out her shortcomings and the methods to correct and remedy them. She was constantly striving for progress. So the current Joan Crawford is no longer Biltie Cassin, who used to be an extra. But people always like to say that she is lucky, and they always underestimate the hardships experienced by successful stars. Of course, there are heroes created by the times. But they gained success without any effort, and they will also lose success without any effort.

Grace Moore, a popular opera star, do you call her lucky? She escaped from a comfortable and wealthy family, not afraid of her parents disowning her, not afraid of hunger, not afraid of the pain of disappointment, just because she was determined to become an opera star. So she lived in a small apartment, singing in small restaurants during the day to earn food, and dancing in small theaters at night. All year round, she followed amateur acting troupes, running around. She also had to save money everywhere to prepare for her opera practice. She slowly rose to the position of leader in comedy, but when she wanted to learn opera, the owner of the Metropolitan Opera told her: "Your throat won't do." But she ignored everything, gave up her superior position in the comedy troupe, and ran to Italy to specialize in opera for two years. When she returned to New York two years later, she was a completely new person. The Metropolitan Opera and all lovers of high-level music bowed down to her. It's because she refused to admit defeat. She may have a natural singing voice, but if she didn't have the courage and determination that nature gave her, she wouldn't have been able to train her singing voice to its current level. From this it can be seen that there are many people in the world who are endowed with glorious singing voices, but those who are not afraid of hardship to train it are as rare as phoenix feathers and unicorn horns.

I can also mention the experiences of several courageous big stars who came out. Ruth Chatterton was originally a pillar of a traveling theater troupe, but she was willing to run up debts and ran to Hollywood to try her luck. As a result, she became the first female star in the sound film era. Maurice Chevalier was booed off the stage and fled by the audience for three consecutive nights when he performed in Paris, but on the fourth night he still took the stage as usual, causing the audience to stand up and cheer for him. Clark Gable was almost starving to death when he first worked as an extra, but he resolutely worked hard and eventually became extremely popular. When Janet Gaynor first arrived in Hollywood, the film company authorities told her that she had nothing attractive and should go home as soon as possible, but she said that she would definitely succeed. As a result, where there is a will, there is a way. Her success has become a good story in film history. Anna Sten used to wash dishes in a small Russian deli in Kiev. But she decided to study acting and was able to come to Hollywood and become a big star who made a splash. People who have seen Helen Hayes's plays say that Helen Hayes is a gifted genius. But she herself tells people about her past hard training and the various hardships she suffered in drama school. People admire Jeanette MacDonald's gorgeous clothes. But Jeanette herself tells people that when she was a dancer, her fellow dancers laughed at her for wearing cotton clothes, and they didn't know that she was unwilling to waste a penny, but saved it to pay for tuition at drama school. As a result, she broke away from the class of dancers, and those who used to laugh at her felt ashamed.

Courage, ambition, and the ability to make decisions are three virtues! In the Hollywood film industry, as in other industries, they are the key to success. We should admire Joan Nede, a new female star. When she was a child, after she had infantile paralysis, people said that she was a cripple for life, but she was unwilling to give up on herself. She practiced dancing, not only became physically strong, but also became a song and dance star. Alice White jumped from a female reporter to a female star. After failing again, she went through all kinds of hardships and has now regained her former position. Gloria Swanson used to be a bather in two-reel comedies and became a first-class star. Greta Garbo was a waiter in a barbershop in Sweden. Charlie Chaplin was a poor child on London's Jewish street and has now become the richest man in the film industry. Wallace Beery was a mahout who looked after elephants when he was a child. Charles Laughton used to be a clerk in a hotel. The rest of the people are too numerous to mention, all of whom have risen from hard work and self-improvement. (The End)

Film Reviews

Review of "Fragrant Wildflowers"

KansasOityPrincess

丨Da Guangming Film Review丨

After watching "Fragrant Wildflowers," it felt like reading a piece of "yellow journalism" embellished and highlighted by reporters at the expense of paper and ink, inevitably leaving one with a sense of "waste."

The story unfolds from the side of two manicurists. Rosanne falls in love with a young hooligan named Dina, while Mary is a manipulative womanizer. Because the former was swindled out of her engagement ring by another hooligan and couldn't face her lover, she disguised herself and blended into the girl scout's special train with the latter to escape to New York. However, Dina caught up with her when she got off the train, so the two jumped into a car in a hurry, flirted with two American country gentlemen in the car, and then followed them onto a mail ship bound for Paris.

What about Dina? He also sneaked onto the ship and became a bodyguard for Alan, a wealthy American who was going to Paris to find his wife. He met the two women again during a manicure opportunity.

Alan suspected that his wife was having an affair with a Russian doctor in Paris, so he specially hired a Parisian detective to investigate. When the detective reported that it was true, he set up a honey trap, using Mary's beauty to seduce the doctor into a trap.

Unexpectedly, the detective used his entrusted task to collude with Mrs. Alan and extort a large sum of money. After Alan lost both money and woman, he fell in love with Mary, and Rosanne and Dina got married.

This inherits the common problems of Hollywood movies: the story is empty, the structure is loose, and the ending is vulgar. We would like to ask, why would a woman like Rosanne prefer Dina? And how could a hooligan like Dina desperately chase after her again and again by plane and ship? Since they loved each other so much, why couldn't one of them explain clearly after losing the ring, and instead just run away? Since the prerequisite for this script's subject matter is empty and unreasonable, it is followed by some accidental and coincidental events, such as Mary and Rosanne meeting American country gentlemen who take them on the ship, Alan hiring a sudden and seemingly kidnapper-like person as a bodyguard, and the reunion during a manicure, and the Russian doctor being easily seduced, all of which are fantasies and nonsense, so the so-called "gags" are not very "funny" at all.

If we were to find some advantages in "Fragrant Wildflowers," it would be the considerable exposure of the "collusion" of so-called lawyers and detectives. On the one hand, they are entrusted to handle a case, and on the other hand, they use the case to collude with the other party, extort money, or "eat oil cakes" from both sides. This is very realistic. Secondly, the way manicurists use crying and laughing to swindle money from gentlemen, and how gentlemen use money to play with women, can also be considered somewhat satirical.

The director was able to achieve this with such an empty script as mentioned above, which is commendable. The play features characters of four nationalities: English, French, American, and Russian. The director's ability to express each person's character and habits in a not-too-exaggerated manner is indeed worthy of praise. Among them, the American gentleman is portrayed most fully, and the few strokes of the Russian doctor are also quite outlined. The weaving between the scenes and the handling of the atmosphere are also very clear and rhythmic.

Joan Blondell's Rosanne and Glenda Farrell's Mary both perform equally hard, but comparatively speaking, the latter performs better. Among the male characters, the one who plays Alan performs more naturally and successfully than the one who plays Dina, even though the latter has a much heavier role than the former.

Audience Opinions

After Watching "Remarriage"

— Fei Nianzu

"Remarriage" is an ordinary story, but it achieved great results in its performance, and can be called a very successful work by the star company.

Of course, the reality of the subject matter and the strictness of the structure are the only elements of the film's success, and the director's consistent efforts are also an undeniable fact. His simple and clear technique is worthy of our praise, especially his great grasp of the portrayal of the characters in the play, and his considerable cleverness in the insertion of several gags: such as college students holding chairs to learn to dance, and returning to school in the middle of the night, climbing over the wall, and fat people accidentally falling into the water tank, which are hilarious.

Actors: Gao Zhanfei played a prodigal son this year, with a glib tongue and a new style. Gao Qianping played a spoiled young girl, performing very realistically, and has made greater progress than in "Daughter's Classic." Yan Yuexian did not achieve special results due to poor makeup, but was generally competent. Xie Yunqing's old country man was lifelike, with amazing results.

Finally, I think that there are too many subtitles, which is an inevitable flaw in this film.

Mother and Daughter Become Sisters

Since "Life," there has been no new work from Lin Chuchu, this typical figure of a virtuous mother and good wife. Recently, it has been decided that she will star in two plays. This is naturally news that people like to hear.

These two plays are "National Customs," co-directed by Luo Mingyou and Zhu Shilin, and "Family Ethics," co-directed by Luo Mingyou and Mu. In both of these films, she plays the mother.

Lin Chuchu is always able to maintain her mother's position in "National Customs," but Ruan Lingyu is not. Because Ruan had played a mother and daughter with Li Lili in "Little Toys," this time, Lin Chuchu became their mother, and Ruan and Li became sisters.

Publication News of Literary Films

Amidst the excitement of magazine years, it is recently heard that a new semi-monthly "Literary Film" will be published in the New Year of 1935. The publication is edited by Ling He and is a comprehensive publication of literary, film, comics, and drama art departments. The first issue includes novels by Ai Wu and Shating, comics by Hu Kao and Chen Jingsheng, a film script by Zheng Junping, and famous works of film and drama by Sun Shiyi, Tang Na, Bao Shi, Zhou Boxun, and Yuan Muzhi. The comic photos are mostly colorfully printed and are very gorgeous. Moreover, the price is low, only fifteen cents per copy.

Film Novel

The Merry Widow (I)

— Suhua

Produced by MGM, starring Jeanette MacDonald and Maurice Chevalier

A majestic mansion stood lifelessly in a small town in the Kingdom of Masovia. Originally, the surroundings of this house were always full of joy. But she 丨Sulia was the unhappiest widow in the world. Masovia is a country that does not compete with the world, and war will never happen. Money? Sulia's property donation is the lifeline of the national economy. But poor 丨丨Masovia's widow! Bound by etiquette, she even had to wear a black and thick veil when going out. She walked listlessly to the lampstand by the bed, opened the drawer and took out her diary. She turned the pages one by one, and a melancholy expression appeared on her slender face at the same time. She turned to the page of July 2, which read: "Dear diary, I am now a widow!" Going down page by page, each page only read: "Nothing is worth writing about!" She sighed, put on her veil and went to the garden. The silver brilliance of the bright moonlight spread across the earth. The intoxicating music from the servants' room made her sit on the stone bench and quietly appreciate it. She looked at the moon and sang a song. When the melancholy singing filled the garden, it was suddenly stopped by a man's singing. She looked over in a hurry and saw a young soldier climbing on the wall. She stood up in panic, and the man had already jumped down, greeting her lightly and saying, "Please don't be alarmed, aren't we all very lonely?" She was about to shout when he took out a letter from his pocket: "An important letter." He said, handing it to her. She secretly looked at him while receiving the letter. A young soldier, with blue eyes and a funny mouth. At that time, he bowed very respectfully and said, "This is a very important letter, I want to wait for a reply." Sulia opened the letter, and she read it, and then slowly read the letter: "Please always think of Tang Erna, he is very alarming." She thought for a while and said, "I don't know who Tang Erna is," he replied in a hurry, "He is Viscount Tang Erna 丨that is me." Sulia asked again, "Who wrote this letter?" The man replied, "I wrote it." Sulia said inexplicably, "I really don't understand, what exactly do you want?" "What I want is just your reply 丨丨" Sulia then ordered him to leave here immediately in an angry tone. She turned to run. But Tang Erna stopped her and said in a gentle voice, begging, "Let me stay a little longer." Sulia straightened her body and glared at him, saying, "I really don't believe that the Royal Guard actually······" "Dares to be wanton towards the most powerful woman. He continued for her. She was really annoyed. He still begged with a hippie smile, "Let you be in my position, if you tell me beautiful lies, and I always wear a veil, then won't you have insomnia at night because of imagining my face?" Sulia listened, furiously pushed him away, and walked towards her house, but Tang Erna still stopped her and asked her to take off the veil. Sulia replied to him with dignity, "Take off the veil? That's possible, but there's no need to take it off now." After she finished speaking, she ran inside without looking back. Tang Erna stood outside the door for a while, straightened his clothes, and then followed in with big strides. On the stairs, Sulia turned to look at this uninvited guest. In the light, he was handsome and extraordinary, indicating that he was a man from Masovia. He looked at her coldly and said, "Madam, I tell you for the last time, our romance is over. Don't think about me anymore. Don't even dream about me." After he finished speaking, he said good night, bowed and left. (To be continued)
